  <script defer="defer" type="text/javascript">
   videojs.Vasq = videojs.Button.extend({
                init: function(player, options){
                        videojs.Button.call(this, player, options);
                        this.on('click', this.onClick);
                }
      });

      videojs.Vasq.prototype.onClick = function() {
        return false;
      };
      
      var createVasqButton = function() {
                var props = {
                        className: 'added-to-control',
                        innerHTML: '&lt;span class="expand-vid" title="Expand"&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'
						 +'&lt;a href="#" class="watch-later-control later-toggle later-toggle-3054" data-cookie="3054" title="Watch Later"&gt;&lt;i class="fa fa-clock-o"&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/a&gt;'
                                                   + ' &lt;div class="prevnext"&gt;'
                                                   +'&lt;a href="http://stockmarketapp.info/cinema/mission-impossible-5-rogue-nation-official-trailer-2015-tom-cruise-spy-movie-1080p-hd/" rel="prev"&gt;&lt;i class="fa fa-backward"&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/a&gt;'
                                                   + '&lt;a href="http://stockmarketapp.info/cinema/avengers-age-of-ultron-roleplay-smyths-toys/" rel="next"&gt;&lt;i class="fa fa-forward"&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/a&gt;'
                                                   +'&lt;/div&gt;'
                                                   +'&lt;a class="target-youtube" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6ws4dYKuZ_A" target="_blank" title="Watch on YouTube"&gt;&lt;i class="fa fa-youtube-play"&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/a&gt;',
                        role: 'button',
                        'aria-live': 'polite',
                        tabIndex: 0
                };
                return videojs.Component.prototype.createEl(null, props);
      };

        var vasq;
        videojs.plugin('vasq', function() {
                var options = { 'el' : createVasqButton() };
                vasq = new videojs.Vasq(this, options);
                this.controlBar.el().appendChild(vasq.el());
        });

        var vid = videojs("single_media_video", {
                plugins : { vasq : {} },
				"controls": true,
								"autoplay": true,
								"preload": "auto",
				"poster" : "http://stockmarketapp.info/wp-content/uploads/2015/05/the-avengers-age-of-ultron-teaser-trailer-discussion-2015-05-213054-860x510.jpg",
				"techOrder":["youtube"],

        });
        
                
        
        (function($){
              'use strict'
              $(document).ready(function(){
		     
		     //WHATSAPP SHARE
		     $('.single-info a.wh').on("click", function(e) {
			    if(/Android|webOS|iPhone|iPad|iPod|BlackBerry|IEMobile|Opera Mini/i.test(navigator.userAgent) ) {
				var article = $(this).attr("data-text");
				var weburl = $(this).attr("data-link");
				var whats_app_message = encodeURIComponent(article)+" - "+encodeURIComponent(weburl);
				var whatsapp_url = "whatsapp://send?text="+whats_app_message;
				window.location.href= whatsapp_url;
			    }else{
				alert('you are not using mobile device.');
			    }
			    e.preventDefault();
		     });
		     
		     
                     $('.tabs-comment .nav-tab a').click(function(e){
                            $('.tabs-comment .nav-tab a').removeClass('on');
                            $('.tabs-comment .item').removeClass('on');
                            $(this).addClass('on');
                            $($(this).attr('href')).addClass('on');
                            e.preventDefault();
                    });
                     $('.single-content-video .head-single a').click(function(e){
                             $(this).toggleClass('closed');
                             $(this).closest('.single-content-video').find('.the-content.format-text').stop().slideToggle();
                             e.preventDefault();
                     });
                      
                      $(document).on('click','.expand-vid',function(){
                             $(this).toggleClass('open');
                             $('.single-video .video-holder').toggleClass('wider');
                     });
                     $('.target-youtube').click(function(){
                            var vid = videojs("single_media_video");
                            vid.pause();
                     });
                     $('.scrollbar-macosx').perfectScrollbar({suppressScrollX:true});
                     $('.tabs-comment .item:first-child').addClass('on');
                     $('.tabs-comment .nav-tab a:first-child').addClass('on');
		                   });

        }(jQuery));
